ka bas dbu mdzad pa'i mkhas btsun mang po dang yon bdag shAkya mgon la sogs pa skye bo'i tshogs du ma dang bcas pa'i dbus su /

shing pho rta'i lo lha ri snying por bzhugs pa'i tshe sgrol mas snye thang du 'byon par bskul nas mthar bla ma dga' ldan du 'byon pa'i bar gyi tshul rnams mgur du bzhes pa 'chi med rdo rje'i glu ste /

bu chos skor la 'brom rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas kyi skyes rabs bstan pa las rngog legs pa'i shes rab kyis zhus pa'i rngog chos nyi shu /
khu chen pos zhus pa'i khu chos gnyis te dril bas nyi shu rtsa gnyis ngo mtshar ba'i gtam thor bu rnams lo tsA ba la sogs pa'i rje'i sras dam pa rnams kyis zur du gleng bas kha bskangs te le'u tha ma /
de ltar glegs bam dngos gzhi le'u bzhi bcu rtsa brgyad /
lo rgyus /
bkod pa phun sum tshogs pa'i gter /
thig le bcu drug /
bka' rgya /
rang rgyud la bskul gdab /
yan lag bdun pa /
'jam dbyangs kyis rngog bskul ba'i tshigs bcad kha bskang ba dang bcas kun dril bas yig sna lnga bcu rtsa drug sogs glegs bam yongs rdzogs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni /
rgya chen spyod rgyud /
zab mo lta rgyud /
nyams len byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa gsum yongs grags ltar la /
brgyud pa gsum chu bo gcig tu 'dres pa jo bo dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na /
'brom ston chos kyi rgyal po /
bshes gnyen gsang phu ba rngog legs pa'i shes rab /
byang chub sems dpa' mnga' ris pa shes rab rgyal mtshan /
phu chung ba gzhon nu rgyal mtshan /
rnal 'byor ka ma pa 'brom rin chen rgyal mtshan /
zhang ston dar ma rgyal mtshan /
stabs ka ba 'brom byang chub bzang po /
ston pa nam mkha' rin chen /
'brom gzhon nu blo gros /
snar thang mkhan po nyi ma rgyal mtshan /
gling kha ba rin chen byang chub /

sge long pa rigs kyi bdag po'i dpal /
sga long pa byang chub dpal /
slob dpon bsod nams 'od zer /
gos sngon chu ser ba sangs rgyas bzang po /
bya bral ba bsod nams bzang po /
bla ma dpal ldan /
stag tshang chos 'khor ba mkhan chen 'od zer /
gnas brtan ye shes tshul khrims /
gnubs chos lung pa mkhan chen rat+na a ka ra shAn+ti /
gnyug la paN chen ngag dbang grags pa /
lo pa spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan /
rje nam mkha' dbang phyug /
chos rje kun dga' legs grub /
lum pa kun dga' chos grags /
mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po /
de dpon mkhyen rab ngag dbang lhun grub /
mtshungs med 'phrin las rnam rgyal /
zhwa lu mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub /
kun mkhyen ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho /
rigs 'dzin 'jam dbyangs grags pa /
rje 'phrin las lhun grub /
rje ngag dbang blo bzang dar rgyas /
rje grags pa rgya mtsho /
rje ngag dbang blo bzang bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan /
rgyal mchog bskal bzang rgya mtsho /
sku mdun mkhan po skal bzang yon tan /
brag ri khyab bdag bde ba'i rdo rje /
mang thos blo bzang tshul khrims /
rje blo bzang thugs rje /
dka' chen ngag dbang mkhas grub /
drin can bla ma skal bzang mkhas grub /
chu bzang bla ma ye shes rgya mtsho /
bka' 'gyur ba dam chos blo bzang /
'dul 'dzin dge 'dun bsod nams /
brag ri blo bzang thub bstan rnam rgyal /
khri sprul ngag dbang blo bzang thub bstan nyi ma /
khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba blo bzang don ldan dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas /
bdag blo bzang ye shes bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho la dgyes bzhin du stsal ba'o / /
jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha nas nye bar brgyud pa'i yi dam gyi lha sna tshogs kyi mngon rtogs rjes gnang man ngag thor bu rnams snar thang mkhan po mchims nam mkha' grags kyis phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i skor la bcom ldan 'das thub pa'i dbang po gtso rkyang gi mngon rtogs /
rjes gnang yod /
rten 'brel gyi gzungs chung /
mnyam med rin chen sgang pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor /
rang khams mi bde ba'i dus bla ma la gsol ba 'debs pa skyer sgang pa las brgyud pa'i @# / /
man ngag /
bla ma'i 'das mchod bya thabs bla ma'i gsung bzhin nam mkha' grags kyis sdebs pa /
des sdebs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das nyan thos kyi tshul bzung nas byang chub sems dpa'i 'phrin las mdzad pa gnas brtan chen po bcu drug la gsol ba btab pa /
rjes gnang yod /
bcom ldan 'das mi 'khrugs pa sprul sku'i cha lugs can gyi mngon rtogs bla ma zhang ston gyi zhal nas byon pa ltar bkod pa /
rjes gnang yod /
thugs rje chen po yi ge drug pa phyag bzhi pa'i mngon rtogs bla ma'i gsung bzhin sdebs pa /
rjes gnang yod /
rje btsun seng+ge sgra'i mngon rtogs mchims nas mchims la brgyud pa'i man ngag bla ma'i gsung las byung ba ltar sdebs /
rjes gnang yod /
thugs rje chen po bcu gcig zhal gtso rkyang gi bzlas lung mngon rtogs zhang pa'i zhal las byung ba ltar dge slong nam mkha' grags kyis sdebs pa /
rjes gnang yod /
yang des sdebs pa'i seng sdeng nags kyi sgrol ma ljang khu gtso rkyang mngon rtogs bla ma'i gsung las byung ba /
rjes gnang yod /
des sdebs pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa sgrub pa'i bar gcod thabs kyis bsrung ba jo mo la gsol ba gdab pa bla ma'i gsung las byung ba /
des sdebs pa'i sgrol ma dkar mo'i tshe bsring ba'i man ngag /
rjes gnang yod /
des sdebs pa'i ri khrod lo ma gyon ma ser mo zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i sgrub thabs /
rjes gnang yod /
des sdebs pa'i lha mo 'od zer can ma phyag gnyis ma'i sgrub thabs /
rjes gnang yod /
zhar byung chom rkun 'ching ba dang bcas pa /
dgra nag nas gsungs pa'i lha mo dbyangs can ma dmar mo zhal gsum phyag drug gi sgrub thabs /
rjes gnang yod /
zhar byung bsnyen sgrub las sbyor dang bcas pa paN+Ti ta su ma ti kI rti nas brgyud pa /
'phags pa 'jam dpal smra ba'i seng+ge dmar ser phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs /
rjes gnang yod /
zhar byung 'jam dbyangs dang dbyangs can ma yab yum la brten pa'i ril bu'i las sbyor /
'phags pa 'jam dpal dkar po'i sgrub thabs /
rjes gnang yod /
zhar byung ma sha'i las sbyor /
dpal dzam b+ha la ser po phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa /
rjes gnang yod /
bgegs mthar byed mthing ga phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs /
rjes gnang yod /
khro bo stobs po che dmar po phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs /
@# / /
rjes gnang yod /
dpal 'byung po 'dul byed phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs /
rjes gnang yod /
sme brtsegs dud kha zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i sgrub thabs /
rjes gnang yod /
khro bo gtum po chen po mi g.yo ba dkar po'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur /
rjes gnang yod /
jo bo mi g.yo ba sngon po'i mngon rtogs bla ma'i gsung bzhin sdebs pa /
rjes gnang yod /
'phags pa mi g.yo ba'i dmigs pa skor gsum bsgom pa'i man ngag /
bcom ldan 'das padma dbang chen phyag gnyis pa'i mngon rtogs bla ma'i gsung las byon pa ltar sdebs pa /
rjes gnang yod /
sku gsung thugs kyi rten la sku khrus gsol ba dge bshes mchad kha ba'i lugs skyer sgang pa las byung ba gtsug gtor 'bar ba'i sgo nas rmi lam mtshan ma ngan pa dang bar gcod zhi ba'i gdams pa bzang po spyod pa'i sgo nas 'chi ba bslu ba'i cho ga skyer sgang pa'i man ngag /
bdag nyid nam 'chi ba gar skye ba sogs brtag pa dpal a ti sha'i gdams pa /
jo bo lugs sats+tshA dgu ma bya thabs jo bo rjes zur rdo rje rgyal mtshan la gnang ba /
rdo rje sems dpa'i yi ge brgya pa jo bo rje dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba /
jo mo gdugs dkar mo can zhal gsum phyag drug ma'i sgrub thabs /
rjes gnang yod /
zhar byung nad pa la phan gdags pa /
phyag na rdo rje mdo lugs sngon po phyag gnyis dpa' bo gcig gi mngon rtogs /
rjes gnang yod /
kha 'bar ma'i gtor ma cha lnga /
kha 'bar ma'i gtor chen jo bo lha gcig nas brgyud pa| klu la gtor ma btang ste 'byor pa sgrub pa'i man ngag /
klu sman dang bcas pa'i klu gtor gyis gnod pa zhi ba'i man ngag /
rgyal po chen po sde bzhi'i gtor ma paN+Di ta dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang /
lo tsA ba dge bshes ston pas bsgyur ba /
rten gtor gyi man ngag bla ma'i zhal las byung ba dge slong chos kyi bla mas yi ger bris pa /
spyan mnga' ba lugs kyi gtor ma brgya rtsa'i man ngag /
'jur 'gegs kyi chu sbyin bya thabs thugs rje chen po kha sar pa Ni'i sgrub thabs /

de'i sgo nas chu sbyin bya thabs /
ngag gi dbang phyug 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs /
rjes gnang yod /
sor 'brang ser mo zhal gsum phyag bcu ma gtso bor gyur pa'i lha mo lnga'i @# / /
sgrub thabs /
rjes gnang yod /
lha mo nor rgyun ma ser mo phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs /
rjes gnang yod /
de'i gzungs kyi man ngag /
rdo rje phag mos dbang du bya ba'i cho ga /
gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma lha dgu'i sgrub thabs bla ma rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa paN+Di ta chos kyi sde dang lo tsA ba dge slong ba ris bsgyur ba /
rjes gnang yod /
byams pa ser po zhal gsum phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs /
rjes gnang yod /
sher phyin ma dkar mo phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs sangs rgyas kyis gsungs pa lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen grags kyis bsgyur ba /
rjes gnang yod /
nor rgyun ma ser mo phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta don yod rdo rje dang lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen grags kyis bsgyur ba /
rjes gnang yod /
khro gnyer can ma ser mo phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs lo tsA ba rin chen grags kyis bsgyur ba /
rjes gnang yod /
rnam sras ljang khu be con can /
rjes gnang yod /
phyag gnyis pa bla ma kha che dgon pa ba'i man ngag gsang ba'i yang snying ma sgrub thabs gnad la 'bab pa'i bla rdo bcas pa gsum gyis bstan pa /
dpal mgon po gri gug mthing nag phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs /

de'i rgyun gtor 'dzin gtor /
mchog sred kyis mdzad pa'i bstod pa /
srin gzugs ma dang bcas pa /

mgon po'i rtags kyi le'u /

ji skad du /
mkhas grub smra ba'i nyi ma dge legs dpal bzang po'i zhal nas /
tshig spyi'i bshad sgrub rtags kyi dge sbyong gis / /

rtags tsam 'dzin pa'i dge sbyong gi spyod pas thub bstan lung rtogs kyi rgya mtsho chen po gang nyid ma rtogs pa dang log par rtog pa'i rnyog ma can du song zhing /

yang gsung 'bum /
kha? pa'i mjug nas gsang 'dus rdzogs rim rim lnga /
bde mchog lU i pa'i rdzogs rim tshigs bcad ma /
de'i dmar khrid zab mo la /
'jigs byed bskyed rdzogs /
yang de'i rdzogs rim /
zhi khro sbrag sgrub rnal 'byor bzhi rim bcas la /
gtor chen drug cu pa'i rnam bzhag la /
chos rgyal phyi sgrub la brten @# / /
pa'i drug cu ma /
de'i zur 'debs myur mgyogs drag po'i pho nya bcas la /
dmag zor mar brten pa'i gdab las /
lcam sring gi bsnyen sgrub drag bskul bcas la /
de ltar bka' rgya ma la khyon bcas yongs rdzogs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni /
rje nyid nas /
rdo rje 'dzin pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan /
rje blo bzang ye shes /
mtsho mdzad dge 'dun don grub /
grub dbang byams pa phun tshogs /
gzim phug blo bzang dge legs /
shar rtse blo bzang yon tan /
rgyal rtse blo bzang phun tshogs /
mkhan blo bzang nyi ma /
rje 'jam dbyangs phrin las /
lho sprul rin po che /
skyabs mgon brag ri rdo rje 'chang /
mchog sprul rin po che blo bzang chos grags rgya mtsho dpal bzang po /
skyabs rje rin po che byams pa bstan 'dzin phrin las rgya mtsho /
des bdag gar gyi dbang po la'o / /
kha pa'i nang gi gsung thor bu dang /
gsan yig /
'od zer sprul sku'i ngor gnang ba dang /
ba so sprul skur gnang ba bcas le tshan bzhi yi lung rgyun ni /

drung pa brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan /
dka' chen bsod nams grags pa /
paN chen blo bzang ye shes /

sngags chen dpal ldan grags pa /
lha btsun don grub rgyal mtshan /
hor sprul chos 'phel bstan 'dzin /
gung sprul mkhyen rab bstan pa'i nyi ma /
rje bka' 'gyur ba blo bzang sbyin pa /
stag brag mchog sprul rin po che /
skyabs rje mchog sprul byams pa bstan 'dzin phrin las rgya mtsho dpal bzang po des /
bdag blo bzang ye shes bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho la'o / /

de nas dngos gung sprul man gong dang 'dra'o / /
! mkhas dang grub pa'i dbang phyug rgyal ba'i 'di chung bzang gsan yig tu lung ma bzhugs pa'i gras su 'dug par rjes su thugs zhib mdzad dgos /
ring lugs pa chen po chen po rje btsun bla ma ngag dbang blo bzang chos ldan dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas la /
dad ldan slob mas bskul ba dang /
rang gi nyams len ched du rje bla ma'i mdo @# / /
sngags kyi gnad dam pa rnams gsal la rgyas par mdzad pa'i gsung rab rnams phyogs gcig tu bsdebs pa'i glegs bam dang po la /
byang chub lam gyi rim pa'i gdams pa tshigs su bcad pa kun mkhyen bde lam la /
skyabs su 'gro ba'i khrid yig rgyas bsdus /
lam rim 'khyer bde /
byang chub lam gyi rim pa'i zhal shes blo bzang lung /
lam rim khrid 'jam dpal zhal lung gi zin bris /
lam khrid kyi sa bcad mdor bsdus lam 'dod smon bcas la /
blo sbyong snyan brgyud chen mo'i rnam bshad gzhan phan nyi ma /
sems pa chen po glang ri thang pas mdzad pa'i blo sbyong tshigs brgyad ma'i khrid yig theg chen dga' ston /
blo sbyong snying po bsdus pa bcas la /
bsag sbyang gi gnad bsdus yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga /
zhing mchog sgo 'byed kyi dmigs rim mdor bsdus /
bde ba can gyi zhing du 'god par byed pa'i myur lam gsal bar byed pa'i sgron me /
smon tshig bkra shis char 'bebs bcas par khyon shog grangs /
glegs bam gnyis par /
phreng ba dang kri ya nas bshad pa'i dkyil 'khor zhe lnga'i ras bris kyi dkyil sgrub cing bsnyen pa bya tshul gyi chog sgrigs blo gsal mgul rgyan nor bu'i phreng ba zhes bya ba la shog grangs /
phreng ba dang kri ya sbrags pa'i dkyil 'khor zhe lnga'i dbang bskur tshul gyi cho ga /
phreng ba gnyis kyi mtha' dpyod rig pa'i 'phrul gyi lde mig ces bya bar shog grangs /
dbang gi sngon 'gro'i lung sbyor /
spyi 'gro'i rjes gnang gi bshad pa mdor bsdus /
mtshan brjod kyi che brjod dang phan yon bshad pa mdor bsdus bcas la / /
yi dam spyi 'gro'i rjes gnang bya tshul blo gsal mgul rgyan la /
rtsa rlung thig le'i rnam gzhag dri ma med pa'i gzhung las 'byung ba btus te bkod pa la /
khyon shog grangs /
'jam mgon bla ma'i gsung gsang rgyud rgyal mchog /
gsang bde 'jigs gsum mngon dkyil la sogs dang / /
bskyed rdzogs zab mo'i lam rim phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa glegs bam gsum par /
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i bla brgyud dang mngon rtogs ngag 'don du bsgrigs pa blo gsal dga' bskyed la /
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i ras @# / /
bris dang bsam gtan gyi dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod bya tshul dngos grub char 'bebs la /
dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i mngon rtogs bde chen gsal ba ngag don bsgrigs pa bde chen rab rgyas la /
'khor lo sdom pa lU i pa'i mdun bskyed sgrub mchod phyi rol mchod pa lag mchod dang bcas pa'i ngag 'don bde chen char 'bebs la /
grub dbang dril bu zhabs lugs kyi bcom ldan 'das 'khor lo sdom pa'i lus dkyil bla brgyud dang mngon rtogs bde chen rab 'phel smon shis bcas pa la /
'khor lo sdom pa lha lnga'i dbang gi brgyud 'debs dang mngon rtogs bde chen char 'bebs bcas la /
bde mchog dril bu'i lus dkyil du dbang bskur ba'i cho ga la /
de'i dbang gi bshad pa la /
'khor lo sdom pa'i tshogs mchod kun bzang mchod sprin dang rgyas pa dang dbang gi sbyin sreg bya tshul bcas la /
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rim pa dang po'i lam la slob tshul gsang chen myur lam rim pa dang po'i gnad don gsal byed nyi ma'i 'od zer bcas par /
'dus pa'i rdzogs rim rgyud don snying po dang dmar khrid blo bzang dgongs rgyan /
rdzogs rim gyi gegs sel bogs 'don gyi man ngag /
'dus pa'i zab gnad gces bsdus bcas la /
dpal 'khor lo sdom pa dril bu lus dkyil gyi rim pa dang po'i khrid dang rdzogs pa'i rim lnga'i dmar khrid bde chen myur lam /
nA ro chos drug las gtum mo'i dmigs rim /
'pho khrid mkha' spyod myur lam bcas par /
dus dgra'i dbang po'i bskyed rdzogs 'jam dpal mnyes byed dang /

zhi gnas sgom tshul /

bcas la /
snying po don gsum gyi khrid yig ga bur chu rgyun /
de'i dmigs rim bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun /
phyag len gyi khrid bcas la /
thabs shes gcod kyi khrid dang nam mkha' sgo 'byed kyi dbang bcas la /
'chi med tshe'i khrid bdud rtsi'i zil mngar /
tshe sgrub 'chi med dga' ston bcas la /
bsnyen yig dngos grub rgya mtsho /
gsang bde 'jigs gsum gyi bsnyen yig dris lan /
mgon po'i bsnyen yig gi yig chung bcas par /
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub thabs za ma tog ngag 'don bya tshul go bde bar bsgrigs pa 'jam dpal dgongs rgyan la /
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po'i sgrub thabs chog bsgrigs kyi 'khrul spong mkhas pa dgyes byed la /
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa'i brgyud 'debs dang /
sgrub thabs bdud las rnam par rgyal ba'i rgyal mtshan /
dpa' bo gcig pa'i mngon rtogs bdud dpung rnam 'joms bcas par /
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgo nas zhi ba'i sbyin sreg bya tshul blo bzang dgongs rgyan shel dkar me long mtha' dyod bcas bde gang 'jigs gsum gyi zhi rgyas kyi sbyin sreg dngos grub rnam gnyis 'gugs pa'i lcags kyu /
rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg sdig ltung mun sel nyi 'od 'bum 'phro bcas la /
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgo nas dge 'dun dbyen bzlums kyi 'khor lo sgrub tshul /
lcags mkhar zur dgu pa'i ngag 'don chog bsgrigs /
glo bur las bcol gyi zor 'phen tshul /

glegs bam lnga par /
rje bla ma ngag dbang mchog ldan dpal bzang po'i rnam thar dad pa'i rol mtsho la /
byin rlabs myur du 'jug byed bla ma lha'i rnal 'byor skor la /
gsol 'debs zhabs brtan skor phyogs gcig tu bkod pa la /
rgyud sde du ma nas gsungs pa'i lha mang po'i mngon rtogs phyogs gcig tu bsdebs pa yi dam rgya mtsho'i sgrub thabs la /
rje bla mar brten pa'i char 'bebs byed tshul la /
dpal rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs pad rag phreng ba'i mdzes rgyan la /
rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi gtor 'bul /
tshogs 'khor bya tshul /
bka' bsgo /
yang gsang gi bsangs mchod bcas la /
ma Ni ril sgrub kyi cho ga 'khyer bde la /
skabs gsum ma'i Tik+ka ngo mtshar dad pa rgyas byed dang /
thog mtha' bar du dge ba'i smon lam gyi Tik+ka legs bshad sgron me bcas par /
rten 'brel snying po'i Tik+ka bde gshegs dgongs rgyan la /
bsnyen rdzogs sogs kyi sdom pa 'bogs chog 'khyer bde kun phan la /
dus chen gyi bshad pa ngo mtshar dga' bskyed la /
sku gsung thugs rten bzhengs pa'i phan yon bshad pa dge legs char 'bebs la /
sku gsung thugs rten bzhengs pa'i dkar chag dang /
bca' yig le tshan bsdoms par /
chos srung dam can rgya mtsho'i gtor 'bul /
'byung bzhi lan chags sogs gtor bsngo'i skor la /
gnam bskos sa'i tshangs pa cing gi sa'i rigs kyi bsrung ma pho lha dung skyong dkar po'i gsol mchod sogs bsangs yig skor la /
lugs gnyis kyi blang dor gsal bar byed pa bslab bya'i skor dang /
bsngo ba /
smon lam 'dod don lhun grub bcas la khyon shog grangs bcas cha tshang gi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni| lho sprul ngag dbang mkhyen rab bstan pa'i dbang phyug yan tshol dgos /
de nas rje bka' 'gyur ba chen po blo bzang don ldan dpal bzang po /

! mkhas grub chen po lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje dpal bzang po'i gsung bka' rgya ma la /
ka? par lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor snyan brgyud las tshogs dang bcas dza pa @# / /
la /
kha? par 'jam dbyangs dang 'brel ba'i zab lam bla ma'i rnal 'byor thun mong ma yin pa dza pa la /
ga? par bde mchog la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor dngos grub 'gugs pa'i lcags kyu la /
nga? par bde mchog lus dkyil dang 'brel ba'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor snyan brgyud shin tu zab sga pa la /
ca? par bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang 'brel ba'i rdzogs rim sgom tshul sgo la /
cha? par bde mchog mkha' spyod mgon po gsum dang 'brel ba'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor dza la /
ja? par dril bu lus dkyil gyi dmar khrid zhal shes la /
nya? par zab lam gtum mo'i khrid yig bde chen rgya mtsho la dza /
ta? par rtsa dbu ma'i nyams len d+hU ti'i gsang thig gi phreng ba la dza /
tha? par bde mchog yab yum la brten pa'i 'pho ba dza la /
da? par rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i bsnyen sgrub kyi rim pa gsal bar bshad pa gsang chen bcu thig la dza /
na? par phag mo'i phreng sngags kyi mchan 'grel la /
pa? par brtag gnyis las byung ba'i rdo rje'i glu'i rnam bshad mkha' 'gro'i zhal lung rdo rje'i gsang mdzod la nga /
pha? par shin tu gsang ba'i mgur dbyangs mkha' 'gro'i snying thig bskul ba'i sgra dbyangs la /
pa? par gnyid mo che'i rmi lam gyi rol mtshor shar ba'i bstan bcos ngo mtshar zla ba'i gzugs brnyan dza la /
ma? par rtsa rlung thig le'i rnam bzhag nya la /
tsa? par dus 'khor lugs kyi rtsa rlung thig le'i rnam bzhag la /
tsha? par ngag byin rlabs la cha /
dza? par tshe sgrub rgyun 'khyer mdor bsdus tshe srog brtan byed rdo rje'i go cha dza la /
wa? par 'chi ang rdo rje'i lha mo'i sgo nas tshe sgrub bya tshul dza /
zha? par 'jigs byed kyi bdag 'jug rgyun 'khyer mdor bsdus la dza /
za? par mgon po snying zhugs dang 'brel ba'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor la dza /
'a? par bla mgon dbyer du gsol ba 'debs pa dngos grub kyi lcags kyu cha la /
ya? par mgon po'i bstod 'phrin bdud las rnam par rgyal ba'i ru mtshon cha la /
ra? par tshe bdag mgon po'i tshe sgrub yid bzhin dbang rgyal dza la /
la? par chos rgyal gyi las gsum rnam @# / /
bzhag rdo rje'i ru mtshon cha la /
sha? par dam can chos kyi rgyal po'i mchod gtor 'phrin bcol gdong lnga sgra dbyangs la dza /
sa? par gshin rje dkar ser dmar gsum gyi bstod 'phrin la lha /
ha? par chos skyong spyi bskul rdo rje'i thog 'bebs la /
dkar chag la bcas khyon bsdoms bzhugs zhes rdo rje 'chang pha bong kha pa byams pa bstan 'dzin dpal bzang pos mdzad pa'i dkar chag 'di nang bzhin gyi rdo rje 'chang stag brag khri sprul rin po che'i phyag dpe'i steng nas legs par thob pa las /
cha rtags can rnams ni /
mdzad pa po lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje /
dza sag dge legs nam mkha' /
lcang lung paN+Di ta ngag dbang blo bzang bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan /
mkhan chen grags pa rgyal mtshan /
sde khri 'jam dbyangs thub bstan nyi ma /
rje blo bzang chos grags rgya mtsho /
lha btsun dngos grub rgyal mtshan /
chu bzang bla ma ye shes rgya mtsho /
bka' 'gyur ba chos 'phel bstan 'dzin /
mkhan chen blo bzang mchog grub /
mkhan chen mkhyen rab bstan pa chos 'phel /
rdo rje 'chang stag brag khri sprul ngag dbang gsung rab mthu stobs bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan /
khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba chen po rje btsun blo bzang don ldan dpal bzang po /
des bdag gar gyi dbang po la dgyes bzhin du stsal ba'o / /

mdzad pa po /
chos rje bstan pa rin chen /

lcang lung man 'dra /
nga rtags can ni /

des bde yangs snyan grags rgya mtsho /
sku 'bum che shod sprul sku byang chub bstan pa'i sgron me /
mkhan chen mkhyen rab bstan pa chos 'phel man 'dra /
dza rtags can ni /

dza sag dge legs nam mkha' /

! mkhas shing grub pa'i dbang phyug thu'u kwan blo bzang chos kyi nyi ma'i gsung 'bum gyi lung ni /
ka? par bla the chen dgongs pa rab gsal gyi rnam par thar pa rin po che'i phreng mdzes la /
grub tha pa'i dbang phyug bkra shis rgya mtsho slob brgyud dang bcas pa'i rnam thar mu tig phreng mdzes la /
grub the dbang ngag dbang rgya mtsho'i rnam thar dpag bsam ljon bzang la /
lcang the skya thams cad mkhyen pa rol pa'i rdo rje'i rnam thar dge ldan bstan pa'i mdzes rgyan gyi stod cha la /
kha? par rnam the thar bstan pa'i mdzes rgyan gyi smad cha la /
rnam thar the dge ldan bstan pa'i mdzes rgyan gyi snyan ngag gi tshigs bcad phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa yang snyan mu tig chun po la /
ga? par gzhon nu nor bzang gi rtogs brjod rgyal sras kun tu dga' ba'i zlos gar la /
dgon lung ma byams pa gling gi dkar chag dpyod ldan yid dbang 'gugs pa'i pho nya la /
ma 'phrin yig me tog gsar pa sna tshogs la /
gzims sa khang dang bsil khang gi rtsigs logs su bris pa snyan tshig 'thor bu la /
nga? par grub sa mtha' thams cad kyi khungs dang 'dod tshul bstan pa legs bshad shel gyi me long le tshan bcu gnyis la /
ca? lam wa rim chen mo'i mchod brjod kyi 'grel sgrigs la /
skyabs khrid mdor bsdus la /
sangs ma rgyas chos tshogs ma'i dmigs rim la /
lam rim sngon 'gro bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi zhal shes thun mong ma yin pa kun mkhyen lam bzang la /
lam rim 'jam dpal zhal lung gi sngon 'gro'i chos gsal bar byed pa blo bzang zhal lung la /
lam sa gyi rim pa'i khrid mdor bsdus nyams su len tshul la /
lam gyi rim pa'i dmigs rnam shin tu bsdus pa gnad don gsal ba la /
lam rim smon lam skal bzang 'jug ngog la /
blo sbyong ma tshigs bcad ma'i khrid yig gces 'dzin gdon 'joms byang sems chu rgyun la /
@# / /
mgur ma 'ga' zhig la /
mgur ma thor bu sna tshogs phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa la /
gsung ma mgur dang zhal gdams thor bu la /
skyabs mgon lcang skya rin po che yab sras kyi gsung mgur la /
gros 'debs snying gi thig le la /
bslab bya snying gtam blang dor rab gsal la /
bslab bya gces pa bco brgyad la /
bslab bya lha'i rnga bo che la /
bslab bya mu tig phreng ba la /
skal bzang bsam 'grub la gnang ba'i bslab bya la /
dam pa'i chos la sgrub pa byed tshul bdud rtsi thig pa la /
bde chen chos gling gi bca' yig bstan pa'i pad tshal rgyas pa'i nyin byed la /
bca' ma yig 'ga' zhig la /
bla ma'i rnal 'byor don gnyis lhun grub kyi dmigs rim dngos grub nor bu 'dren pa'i shing rta la /
sa rgyan sa sbyar nas nyams su len tshul theg chen lam bzang gsal ba'i nyi ma la /
zhabs ra brtan gsol 'debs dge legs 'dod 'jo'i 'grel ba me long la /
'jam ma dbyangs bzhad pa dgung lo bdun skabs su gnang ba'i tshigs bcad don 'grel la /
thar sa pa chen po'i mdo 'don pa'i cho ga 'khrul sel blun po'i kha la rgyas 'debs la /
rje btsun dam sa pa rang byung ye shes rdo rjes mdzad pa'i ma Ni'i sgrub thabs kyi 'grel pa don bzang lta ba'i mig 'byed la /
rje btsun dam pa rang byung ye shes rdo rje'i gsol 'debs byin rlabs sgo 'byed la /
rje btsun pa blo bzang chos kyi nyi ma'i 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs le tshan la /
'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs dang zhabs brtan skor la /
bla ma ma du ma'i zhabs brtan skor la /
'jam sa dbyangs gong ma'i zhabs brtan dge legs 'dod 'jo sogs la /
myur ma byon skor la /
cha? par bla ma'i rnal 'byor dngos grub bum bzang la /
zab lam bla ma'i rnal 'byor mdor bsdus la /
bla ma'i sa rnal 'byor dngos grub char 'bebs la /
sgrol dkar gyi bla ma'i rnal 'byor la /
rnam rgyal ma'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor la /

la /
rta mgrin gsang ka sgrub kyi 'khor lo'i man ngag gi zin tho gter gyi kha byang lta bu la /

glegs bam bzhengs tshul mthong grol ngo mtshar ltad mo la /

rje btsun ku ru ka ru {ka} l+le'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga khams gsum dbang du sdud pa'i lcags kyu la /
dpal {ka} ldan dmag zor rgyal mo'i gtor chen thun mong ma yin pa'i man ngag gsal bar bkod pa dgra srog gcod pa'i spu gri la /
myur {ka} mdzad ye shes mgon po phyag drug pa'i gtor chen gyi man ngag nag po 'gro shes su bkod pa sdig can sgrol ba'i spu gri ngar ma la /
dpal ldan ka lha mo dmag zor ma'i bsnyen sgrub kyi man ngag snying po bcud bsdus la /
'dod {ka} khams dbang phyug dpal ldan dmag zor rgyal mo'i drag po'i gtor chen gyi cho ga bdud dpung 'joms pa'i rdo rje la /
dam ka can chos kyi rgyal po phyi nang gsang gsum gyi bsnyen pa bya tshul sbyin sreg dang bcas pa bai DUr+ya'i phreng ba la /

chos skyong rgyal ka po sku lnga'i bsnyen pa bya tshul rgyal po rol mtsho la /

! khri chen brgyad kyi dmigs rim skyong tshul rgya ra chos skyong bzang po'i gsung rgyun bya btang d+harma ki rtis yi ger bkod pa la /
sog po 'jam dbyangs 'phrin las kyis mtshan bu btab pa 'bras spungs par ma'i steng nas mchan bu ma gtogs gzhan thams cad kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni /
khri grags pa don grub yan de'i gsan yig ltar la /
de nas mkhan chen bstan pa chos 'phel /

des bdag gar dbang la'o / /
! spos dkar sprul sku'i gsung ma mo'i 'khrugs skong bya tshul nyes pa kun sel gyi lung brgyud ni /

tre hor bka' 'gyur ba blo bzang sbyin pa /

des bdag blo bzang ye shes bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho la'o / /
